Monte-Carlo Paths

Contents

  • VG initial parameters
  • Compute CGM variables for two gamma;s
  • Compute the path
  • CIR and IntCIR

VG initial parameters

s0 = 100; T=1; rfr = 0.0421; dy = 0.0311; n=250;
nu = 0.67514; sigma = 0.21; theta = -0.1368;
omega = log(1-sigma^2* nu/2 - theta * nu)/nu;

Compute CGM variables for two gamma;s

C = 1/nu;
G = (sqrt(theta^2*nu^2/4+sigma^2*nu/2) - theta * nu/2)^(-1);
M = (sqrt(theta^2*nu^2/4+sigma^2*nu/2) + theta * nu/2)^(-1);

Compute the path

times

dt = T/n;
% the path
[s,t] = vgprcg1g2(s0,dt,T,rfr,dy,omega,C,G,M);
% plot the path
plot(t,s);
xlabel('Time');
title('Variance Gamma G1 - G2');

CIR and IntCIR

T =1; n=250; dt = T/n;
kappa =0.5; eta = 1; lambda = 0.8; y0=1.2;
[cir,icir,tt]=cirprc(y0,dt,T,kappa,eta,lambda);
plot(tt,icir,'b',tt,cir,'r',tt,eta,'y')
legend('IntCIR','CIR','\eta');
